    function carregaMenuSeg() {
      var chk = localStorage.getItem("LCMenuSeg");
      if (chk != null) {
        var obj = JSON.parse(chk);
        for (var x = 0; x < obj.length; x  ) {
          $("#menuSeg"   (6 - x)).html('<a href="'   obj[x].link   '">'   obj[x].categoria   '</a>');
        }
      }
    }

  });
